<CodeSampleTab

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-list_deployments_v1_workflows_deployments_get_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.deployments.listDeployments({});

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-list_deployments_v1_workflows_deployments_get_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-list_deployments_v1_workflows_deployments_get_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.deployments.list_deployments(active_only=True)

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"

  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-get_deployment_v1_workflows_deployments_name_get_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.deployments.getDeployment({
    name: "<value>",
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-get_deployment_v1_workflows_deployments_name_get_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-get_deployment_v1_workflows_deployments_name_get_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.deployments.get_deployment(name="<value>")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/workflows/deployments/\{name\}/logs \{#operation-get_deployment_logs\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Obtenir les logs d'un déploiement_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Récupérer les logs d'un déploiement (tous ses workers).

Utilisez `after`/`before`/`order` lors de la première requête pour définir la plage temporelle et l'ordre de tri ; pour les pages suivantes, transmettez le `cursor` de la réponse précédente (il mémorise la plage et l'ordre).

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-get_deployment_logs_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-get_deployment_logs_code-samples_typescript">

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.deployments.getDeploymentLogs({
    name: "<value>",
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-get_deployment_logs_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-get_deployment_logs_code-samples_python">

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.deployments.get_deployment_logs(name="<value>", order="asc", limit=50)

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-get_deployment_logs_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-get_deployment_logs_code-samples_curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/workflows/deployments/{name}/logs \
 -X GET \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APIKEY_HERE'
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/workflows/deployments/\{name\}/logs/stream \{#operation-stream_deployment_logs\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Diffuser les logs d'un déploiement_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Diffuser les logs d'un déploiement (tous ses workers) via SSE.

Le curseur de reprise provient de l'en-tête `Last-Event-ID` ou du paramètre de requête `last_event_id` (l'en-tête est prioritaire) et prévaut sur `after` ; omettez tous les paramètres pour suivre depuis le début du déploiement.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-stream_deployment_logs_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-stream_deployment_logs_code-samples_typescript">

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.deployments.streamDeploymentLogs({
    name: "<value>",
  });

  for await (const event of result) {
    console.log(event);
  }
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-stream_deployment_logs_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-stream_deployment_logs_code-samples_python">

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.deployments.stream_deployment_logs(name="<value>")

    with res as event_stream:
        for event in event_stream:
            # handle event
            print(event, flush=True)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-stream_deployment_logs_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-stream_deployment_logs_code-samples_curl">

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/workflows/deployments/{name}/logs/stream \
 -X GET \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APIKEY_HERE'
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>
